q0#####SELECT lineitem.l_discount,lineitem.l_extendedprice,nation.n_name   FROM   customer AS customer, lineitem AS lineitem, nation AS nation, orders AS orders, region AS region, supplier AS supplier  WHERE customer.c_custkey = orders.o_custkey AND customer.c_nationkey = supplier.s_nationkey AND lineitem.l_orderkey = orders.o_orderkey AND lineitem.l_suppkey = supplier.s_suppkey AND nation.n_regionkey = region.r_regionkey AND supplier.s_nationkey = nation.n_nationkey AND (orders.o_orderdate >= '1997-01-01'::date) AND (orders.o_orderdate < '1998-01-01 00:00:00'::timestamp without time zone) AND (region.r_name = 'ASIA'::bpchar);
q1#####SELECT nation.n_name,part.p_mfgr,part.p_partkey,supplier.s_acctbal,supplier.s_address,supplier.s_comment,supplier.s_name,supplier.s_phone   FROM   nation AS nation, part AS part, partsupp AS partsupp, region AS region, supplier AS supplier  WHERE nation.n_regionkey = region.r_regionkey AND part.p_partkey = partsupp.ps_partkey AND supplier.s_nationkey = nation.n_nationkey AND supplier.s_suppkey = partsupp.ps_suppkey AND ((part.p_type)::text ~~ '%BRASS'::text) AND (part.p_size = 45) AND (region.r_name = 'AMERICA'::bpchar);
q2#####SELECT lineitem.l_discount,lineitem.l_extendedprice,n2.n_name,orders.o_orderdate   FROM   customer AS customer, lineitem AS lineitem, nation AS n1, nation AS n2, orders AS orders, part AS part, region AS region, supplier AS supplier  WHERE customer.c_nationkey = n1.n_nationkey AND lineitem.l_orderkey = orders.o_orderkey AND n1.n_regionkey = region.r_regionkey AND orders.o_custkey = customer.c_custkey AND part.p_partkey = lineitem.l_partkey AND supplier.s_nationkey = n2.n_nationkey AND supplier.s_suppkey = lineitem.l_suppkey AND ((part.p_type)::text = 'ECONOMY BRUSHED BRASS'::text) AND (orders.o_orderdate >= '1995-01-01'::date) AND (orders.o_orderdate <= '1996-12-31'::date) AND (region.r_name = 'ASIA'::bpchar);
q3#####SELECT customer.c_acctbal,customer.c_address,customer.c_comment,customer.c_custkey,customer.c_name,customer.c_phone,lineitem.l_discount,lineitem.l_extendedprice,nation.n_name   FROM   customer AS customer, lineitem AS lineitem, nation AS nation, orders AS orders  WHERE customer.c_custkey = orders.o_custkey AND customer.c_nationkey = nation.n_nationkey AND lineitem.l_orderkey = orders.o_orderkey AND (lineitem.l_returnflag = 'R'::bpchar) AND (orders.o_orderdate >= '1995-01-01'::date) AND (orders.o_orderdate < '1995-04-01 00:00:00'::timestamp without time zone);
q4#####SELECT lineitem.l_discount,lineitem.l_extendedprice,lineitem.l_shipdate,n1.n_name,n2.n_name   FROM   customer AS customer, lineitem AS lineitem, nation AS n1, nation AS n2, orders AS orders, supplier AS supplier  WHERE customer.c_custkey = orders.o_custkey AND customer.c_nationkey = n2.n_nationkey AND orders.o_orderkey = lineitem.l_orderkey AND supplier.s_nationkey = n1.n_nationkey AND supplier.s_suppkey = lineitem.l_suppkey AND ((n1.n_name = 'SAUDI ARABIA'::bpchar) OR (n1.n_name = 'RUSSIA'::bpchar)) AND ((n2.n_name = 'RUSSIA'::bpchar) OR (n2.n_name = 'SAUDI ARABIA'::bpchar)) AND (lineitem.l_shipdate >= '1995-01-01'::date) AND (lineitem.l_shipdate <= '1996-12-31'::date);
q5#####SELECT lineitem.l_discount,lineitem.l_extendedprice,lineitem.l_quantity,nation.n_name,partsupp.ps_supplycost   FROM   lineitem AS lineitem, nation AS nation, orders AS orders, part AS part, partsupp AS partsupp, supplier AS supplier  WHERE orders.o_orderkey = lineitem.l_orderkey AND part.p_partkey = lineitem.l_partkey AND partsupp.ps_partkey = lineitem.l_partkey AND partsupp.ps_suppkey = lineitem.l_suppkey AND supplier.s_nationkey = nation.n_nationkey AND supplier.s_suppkey = lineitem.l_suppkey AND ((part.p_name)::text ~~ '%dark%'::text);
